Local News of This City

Completion of Dike Project by the National Government Flood Relief Committee

All engineers are Chinese, none are Westerners; a grand ceremony was held in Nanjing today. The inspection committee set off by ship the day before yesterday, starting from Zhenjiang, scheduled to complete in one month.

Since its establishment last year, the National Government Flood Relief Committee, in addition to distributing emergency relief and agricultural assistance, also planned large-scale work relief projects. The seven provinces most severely affected by the disaster were divided into eighteen districts. Work began last winter. Now, except for one or two places where completion was impossible due to special circumstances and which were transferred to the National Economic Council for continued handling, all the others have been completed one after another. The main dikes of the rivers Jiang, Huai, Gan, Han, Yi, Luo, Li, and Yun have all been repaired and completed. Now the National Government Flood Relief Committee is about to conclude all its work within the year, having spent a total of about 60 million yuan on emergency relief, agricultural assistance, and work relief. The work relief aspect accounts for over 20 million yuan. The project was vast, so a Dike Project Inspection Group was specially organized, inviting ministers from various ministries and leaders from Chinese and Western communities in Shanghai to participate. A completion ceremony was held in Nanjing on the 18th. The inspection group left Shanghai on the morning of the 16th at 10 o'clock aboard the China Merchants Bureau's special Jiangxin steamer. The planned inspection route starts from Zhenjiang, goes west along the Yangtze River through Nanjing, Wuhu, Datong, Anqing, Pengze, Jiujiang to Hankou, then turns from Han to Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Bengbu, Gaoyou, Yancheng, Funing, Dongtai, and then returns to Shanghai. The inspection period is scheduled for one month. As for the inspection group for bandit areas in the four provinces of Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui, invited by Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang, there is no confirmed organization in Shanghai yet. One or two representatives from other groups also joined the ship to Hankou. It is expected that after another thorough discussion in Nanjing, they will arrive in Hankou to meet Chairman Chiang for instructions, and then formulate detailed inspection methods. In fact, the inspection group and the inspection group are one and two, and those who are. A reporter from this newspaper is also one of the participants. The details of leaving Shanghai and arriving in Zhenjiang are recorded below. The findings of inspections along the way will be published in succession.

The Situation of Leaving Shanghai

The organization of the Dike Project Inspection Group was prepared by Committee Member Li Zujin at the request of Song Ziwen, Chairman of the Flood Relief Committee. Representatives from all walks of life participated enthusiastically, but temporarily, due to important official duties, many changed to taking the evening train to Nanjing on the 17th to attend the completion ceremony, such as Yu Youren, Wang Xiaolai, Li Zujin, and Liu Yunfang. Some withdrew directly due to their own affairs, such as Liu Zhanen and Wang Yansong, so there were many changes in the representatives. The Jiangxin steamer was specially chartered by the Flood Relief Committee, and the reception matters were handled jointly by staff members of the Flood Relief Committee, Shi Shiliang and Shi Bangrui. The ship left Shanghai at 10:45 a.m. on the 26th. Li Zujin and other staff members of the Flood Relief Committee went to the Jinliyuan Wharf to see them off.

Representatives from All Walks of Life

The representatives from all walks of life who set off from Shanghai that day included Song Zi'an representing Song Ziwen, Lin Kanghou representing the Bankers' Association, Wen Lanting representing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Wu Rulin representing the Money Dealers' Association, Luo [Blank] Hui representing Mayor Wu, Wu Shan representing the Roads Association, and Mr. and Mrs. Hu Junzhuang, Mr. and Mrs. Hu Xuanming, Mr. and Mrs. Fei Wusheng, Wu Liande, and reporters from Chinese and Western newspapers, including Qian Hua from Shen Bao, Lu Yi from Xinwen Bao, Zhu Yunguang from Shishi Xinbao, Fei Enqu from Zi Lin Xi Bao, and reporters from Chinese and Western news agencies. On the National Government Flood Relief Committee side, there were Chairman Simpson, Committee Member Zhang Shouyong, Work Relief Office Director Xi Dejiong, General Affairs Office Zhou Qibang, and over sixty engineers and other staff members.

Inspection Schedule

The inspection schedule is divided into two major parts. From November 26th to December 8th, it is the first part, inspecting the main dike project of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Jianghan. From December 21st to October 24th, it is the first part, inspecting the Yi, Luo, Huai, and Yun projects in southern Henan, northern Anhui, and Lixiahe. As for the detailed schedule, it will depart from Shanghai on the 26th, arrive in Zhenjiang on the 17th, and inspect the dike projects at the river mouth and Tongjing. On the 28th, it will arrive in Nanjing and hold the completion ceremony at the Flood Relief Association at 3:00 p.m. On the 29th, it will be in [Blank] Lake Datong, on the 30th in Anqing [Blank] Ze, on December 1st in Jiujiang Nanchang, and on the 1st in Huangshigang Hankou. After arriving in Hankou, the schedule will be rearranged and transferred to Zhengzhou, [Blank] City, Luoyang, and return to Bengbu, [Blank] Tai, Zhengyangguan, Gaoyou, Qingjiangpu, [Blank] City, Funing, [Blank] Tai, and then return to Shanghai. It is heard that representatives from all walks of life are scheduled to return after arriving in Hankou.

Xi Dejiong's Speech

Xi Dejiong, Director of the Work Relief Office, said to reporters on the ship: "I, Dejiong, was ordered to handle the work relief, but I am very afraid because of my mediocre talent. According to the great flood last year, the population affected by the disaster in the southeastern provinces was more than 50 million, and the area affected by the disaster reached 400,000 square li. After eight or nine months of hard work, more than one million disaster workers were recruited, and thousands of engineers and technical staff were hired. Only then was the work relief in various districts completely completed. It is found that the matter of work relief is to use work to replace relief. The disaster workers can get relief through work, and the country can revitalize industry. The relationship is extremely complex. Although the name of work relief often appears in historical records, the methods are not detailed, and it is not known exactly. Therefore, there were no successful methods to refer to when handling this work relief, and the time was also very short. The difficulties can be imagined. Later, fortunately, with the support of all parties, there was some success, which was really a fluke. However, how is the work area, after all, the actual work site, and what is the truth? The outside world still has some misunderstandings. Therefore, on the occasion of the completion of the great work, I respectfully invite people from all walks of life, Chinese and foreign, to conduct on-site inspections in various districts for guidance. Gentlemen of the press, you have always been in the position of teachers of the people. I have long planned to invite you to gather and report all the handling situation, but because of the busy affairs, I have not been able to do so. At this Chinese and foreign dike project inspection meeting, I specially sincerely invite you to go together. My intention is very serious. After you have conducted on-site inspections of how vast the disaster area was last year, how tragic the disaster situation was, and how difficult the work relief was, you can fully understand it. You can use what you have learned to offer it to the world, so that people in the world can understand the situation of the work relief handled this year, and its benefits to the national economy and people's livelihood are extremely important. Moreover, Dejiong has greater hopes for you. You must know why China has floods every year, and why the disaster last year was so serious. Although it can be said to be God's will, it is not necessarily caused by the failure of people to repair things on weekdays. Just look at how many rivers and channels pay attention to rectification? Once something happens, they are at a loss. This can be taken as a warning. This year, the country has spent tens of millions of huge sums of money, borrowed American wheat, and built dikes of 7,000 or 8,000 kilometers, and dredged hundreds of kilometers of rivers and channels. From now on, the people and governments of all provinces must take care of them and repair them from time to time so that they can last. Otherwise, after a few years, they will be destroyed again. I hope you will explain this idea to the local people in a kind and sincere way, so as to avoid the recurrence of floods. The inspection time is only set for more than 30 days. With more than 10,000 li of long dikes, of course, only the important sections can be seen, and it is impossible to see them all in detail. However, for this inspection, the National Government Flood Relief Association, although the time is short, the meaning is extremely long. Now we are sailing upstream along the river. Wherever we go, Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Wuhu, Jiujiang, Hankou, and Xin Dike and Jianli, we will inspect the Yangtze River dikes. After returning [Blank], we will go to Xiantao Town and Yuekou area to inspect the Han River project. We will also go from Hankou to Zhengzhou to inspect the Yi, Luo, and Sha Ying rivers, stone and earthworks. Then we will go from Zhengzhou to Bengbu to inspect the work relief in the three districts of Anhui and Huai. Finally, we will go to the northern part of Jiangsu to inspect the canal and Lixiahe dike drainage projects. The long journey is arduous. I sincerely hope that you will not spare your efforts and carry things through to the end. I am very fortunate. This [Blank] work, the time is short and hurried, and the reception is not good. Please forgive me. If you have any questions, please contact engineers Zhang Chongji and Xue Zhaoshu of our office at any time. I will sincerely tell you everything, and I still hope to be taught from time to time."

Evening Gathering

At 8:30 p.m. on the 26th, the entire inspection group gathered in the dining room of the Jiangxin steamer. Chairman Simpson of [Blank] presided over the meeting. Simpson's Speech

Vice Chairman Simpson said at the time, "It is a great honor for you to come. I have several thoughts on the work of the Flood Relief Association. First, the economic impact. Millions of disaster victims in the disaster area have been given a new lease of life because of the relief work of the Flood Relief Association, and the construction of dikes has made it possible for the rural economy to recover as soon as possible. This year's good harvest should be attributed to this. In terms of China's entire national economy, the disaster area [Blank] and the disaster victims are greatly affected. First, the political impact. Most of the disaster areas are based in the Communist Party. If the government does not provide relief, millions of disaster victims will invest in the Communist Party, which will be endless. Moreover, because the Central Government directly sets up associations to distribute relief, it makes the villagers think about the kindness of the National Government, and indirectly disperses the efforts of the Communist Party, until they are exhausted and powerless. Third, we should pay special attention to the fact that the entire dike construction project of the Work Relief Office of the Association is completely undertaken by Chinese engineers, and no Westerners participate in it, breaking the usual practice, which is very commendable. Fourth, recently [Blank] all parties have quite a few unsatisfactory criticisms of this association. It should be known that no matter what [Blank] things, it is impossible to be completely satisfactory. We hope [Blank] you will give strict criticism after inspecting the various projects, and hope to conclude after the inspection [Blank], that is, the Flood Relief Association [Blank] more than 60 million yuan, in terms of today's achievements, is it worth it?"

Zhang Shouyong's Speech

At that time, I and Mr. Rong Zongjing met with Finance Minister Song, and took the American wheat loan as a key point of discussion. After consideration, because the disaster was too widespread, we had to seek help from countries around the world. To make up for the deficiency with their surplus is not contradictory in terms of [Blank] and reason. Therefore, we proceeded resolutely until it was successful. Domestic circles and overseas Chinese successively donated more than 8 million yuan. The Flood Relief Association has today's achievements, all thanks to the gifts of countries around the world and various circles. This should be specially thanked to you, especially the foreign guests present. Now that the dike has been completed, we especially hope that we will work hard to request good follow-up methods for the dike, that is, how to make the dike permanent and not damaged. In my opinion, the most important thing is to ask the central government to enact a dike protection law, and at the same time, the Ministry of Finance should [Blank] set up a dike tax to be used for repairs at any time, so that it can be done once and for all. Inspection of the First District

The Jiangxin steamer arrived in Zhenjiang at around 4:00 a.m. on the 27th [Blank]. Because the wharf was not repaired [Blank], it was anchored in the heart of the river. At 8:00 a.m., Han Deqin, a member of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Li [Blank] Yang, the head of the Security Department, took the Jiangli ferry to the ship to [Blank] greet them. At the same time, Li [Blank], a staff member of the Lizi [Blank], also rushed from Nanjing to take care of things. At 3:00 p.m., a completion ceremony for the dike project will be held in the Jiangxin steamer's cabin, and ministers from various ministries and consuls from various countries will be invited to participate. At 8:30 a.m., the whole party transferred to the Jiangli ferry to the opposite bank to inspect the dike project of the first district. Xue Zhaoshu, the head of the first district project, led the [Blank]. The ferry [Blank] arrived at the river bank [Blank] and changed to a public bus. After traveling about one mile to Hongqiao Town, they got off the bus and walked half a mile to Dazaoganzhou Dike, which is the starting point of the Flood Relief Association's dike project. Most of the old dike of Dazaoganzhou [Blank] had collapsed. Now a new dike has been built. Looking at the old dike from a distance, it is like the first line of defense, and the new dike is the second line of defense. It is about four-tenths of a foot high, one meter higher than the flood level last year, and about six-tenths of a mile long. Vegetables have been planted on both sides of the dike, with green and yellow alternating, endless at a glance. According to the staff of the Engineering Office, this dike is the simplest of all, and the most people working on it reached 7,000 or 8,000, and at least 1,000. The dike soil was all dug from the people's fields next to it, to a depth of 4 meters, and now it is full of stream water, looking like a fishing pond. Then they went to Guadong Dike for inspection. Along the way, the responsible [Blank] project specialists gave detailed explanations. Guadong Dike is [Blank] lower than Dazaoganzhou Dike. There are only more than 20 earthen houses built on the dike as temporary homes for disaster victims. They are very busy at work, and men and women help each other, which is very harmonious. According to the villagers, in last year's flood, the water reached [Blank], and all the property was swept away by the flood, but fortunately, no lives were sacrificed, which is gratifying. This year's harvest is good, but the price of grain has fallen, which is not profitable. At 11:00 a.m., the whole party took the Jiangli ferry back to the Jiangxin steamer for a short rest, and then had lunch to respond to the joy of the Jiangsu Provincial Government.

Prior Planning

A reporter from Xin Sheng She, along with Section Chief [Blank] Mingjiu, and engineers Xue Zhaoshu and Lu Chao, had detailed discussions on the ship about the work relief process, and received detailed answers, which are recorded as follows: The design of water conservancy projects cannot be done without a long-term overall plan, but our country's restoration after fatigue is especially difficult. From the national level to the provincial and county levels, although water conservancy organizations are everywhere, there are many huge plans, but the implementation is few. The Work Relief Office of the Flood Relief Association, in order to relieve disaster victims, could not wait. The plan should be practical. As soon as the water receded, construction should begin immediately. The outline of the design is described as follows:

Construction Standards: In the flood area last year, from Dongting Lake and Poyang Lake in the south, to the main streams of the Jianghuai, Hanyun, and Feihe rivers in the central part, and the banks of the rivers and dams of the Tuo, Hao, Yi, and Luo rivers in the north, up to thousands of miles, it is impossible to repair them all due to lack of financial resources. Therefore, six construction standards were formulated based on economic conditions and relief needs: 1. The scope of work relief is limited to earthworks, and the types of projects are mainly the repair of main dikes and supplemented by river dredging to discharge water. 2. Dike repair should focus on the parts of the main rivers that were flooded and breached in the current flood. 3. The restoration should be to the original state or able to resist floods like the current flood. 4. The dilapidated or waterway-obstructing parts of the old dike may be slightly modified, such as raising, thickening, moving the bay, and straightening. 5. For the dilapidated old dikes where the earthwork does not exceed the repair, new dikes may be built as appropriate. 6. For the purpose of draining accumulated water, the original river channels may be opened up or connected. For the Yangtze River embankments, they should be repaired from Zhenjiang and above based on the flood situation last year.

Surveying Process: After the establishment of the Flood Relief Association, it chartered an airplane and, in August last year, requested the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Yangzhoujiang Remediation Committee to send personnel to take the plane to survey the disaster areas of the Yangtze River and the Dongting and Poyang lakes. The flood area of the Grand Canal was surveyed by General Zhu Lianlan, director of the disaster area working group, and Zhou Xiangxian and others by plane. In late October, when the water receded slightly, the Yangzhoujiang Waterway Remediation Committee, the Huai River Guidance Committee, the Construction Departments of Hunan and Jiangsu provinces, and the Water Conservancy Bureaus of Hubei and Jiangxi provinces were convened to survey the Jianghan Huaiyun, Xiangchen Lake, and Gan various water dikes separately, so that there was a basis for project estimates and construction plans.

Dike Standards: Dike projects are divided into repair and new construction. According to the regulations of the Technical Committee of the Flood Relief Association, the height should be one-tenth of a foot higher than the flood level, the dike surface should be 3 meters to 4 meters wide, and the slope on both sides should be 1:3 for the outer slope. The dike is ten feet high and the slope is 20 feet long, and the inner slope is 1:5, which is a great improvement compared to the old dike, which only had a slope of 1:1. It also formulated 20 dike construction guidelines, including dike [Blank] soil research (compact new soil with stone hammer), acceptance supervision, (such as preventing the disadvantages of wearing hats and boots, that is, only adding the top of the dike and the [Blank] of the dike, etc.,) and other items, all have detailed regulations, and six dike construction drawings, detailing the soil excavation grid to avoid digging into the river, and the construction of roads across the dike, and the first slope along the river bank should follow the river and go down, and should not be parallel against the flow, or form right angles, etc.

River Dredging Plan: The Lixiahe area in Jiangsu (Yancheng, Yuhua, and Donghao counties) is shaped like the bottom of a pot. Whenever there is a big flood, the Jiang and Huai rivers cannot accommodate it and converge here. The original five ports are winding and silted up. Therefore, the five ports of [Blank] Xiahe, as well as the Yuanhe and Shahe rivers in eastern Henan, and the Beifei rivers between Huai and Si, should be dredged, the silt should be dredged, the bends should be straightened, and the blockages should be cleared to discharge the accumulated water. The slope of the river bank varies from place to place, but is generally 1:2.5, and there are also 1:3 and 1:1.

Construction Process

The Engineering Office [Blank] belongs to the Disaster Area Working Group, with Xi Mingjiu as the director, divided into two sections, engineering and technology, and eighteen work relief bureaus outside. It was originally scheduled to end in June this year, but because several projects were not completed, it was extended to September. A small number of unfinished projects were transferred to the Jinguo Economic Committee for handling.

Setting up bureaus by district is for the convenience of implementation and management. According to the size of the river system and the severity of the disaster, it is divided into eighteen districts in total, including seven districts in the Yangtze River, three districts in the Huai River, two districts in the Han River, three districts in the Lixiahe, one district in each of the Xiangyuan, Yi Luo, and Su Yun rivers. Except for the [Blank] Xiahe [Blank] fifteen districts, due to changes in the plan, only three sections were handled, divided into the sixteenth and seventh districts, and the tenth district of Xiangyuan was entrusted to the Hunan Flood Relief Rehabilitation Association to handle it on its behalf. The remaining sixteen districts all established engineering bureaus, each with an engineer as the director and deputy engineer, technicians, clerks, etc. Below the district, depending on the size of the project, it is divided into several sections, each with a deputy engineer as the section chief and technicians and clerks. Below the section is divided into ten regiments, each with an overseer and a deputy overseer, and the labor regiment is divided into twenty rows, each with twenty-five disaster workers, selecting the most capable as the row head.

Wheat Wages: The Flood Relief Association lent 450,000 tons of wheat from the United States, of which 30 million tons were used for work relief. The number of allocations in each district was determined by the Technical Committee after surveying and estimating the closure of each district. General wheat stations were set up in Pukou, Wuhu, Anqing, Hankou, and Jiujiang, and one, two, or three class stations were set up at his discretion. The transportation team was responsible for transporting, storing, and distributing affairs officers. Disaster victims are paid wages according to the amount of earthwork they do. The payment standards are: 1. Flat land soil extraction is 25 cents to 40 cents per square meter. 2. If the soil extraction is more than 50 meters away, add 5 cents per square for every 20 meters. For deep soil extraction and high soil dropping, add 3 cents per square for every meter high or deep. 3. For ramming work, one corner per square. Every week, the technicians and supervisors check and accept the earthwork once and fill out a wheat voucher, which the head of the row takes to the grain station to collect.

Page 10

Repairing Dikes: The Flood Relief Association's use of work for relief to repair dikes accounts for [Blank] half of the entire project. Therefore, except for the sixteenth and seventeenth districts, which are river dredging, and the tenth and twenty-eighth districts, most of which are river dredging, the rest are dike construction. The Dongting Lake system in the [Blank] district is handled by the Lake and Water Disaster Committee on its behalf, completing 9,426,050 cubic meters of earthwork, issuing 20,000,000 tons of wheat, and repairing [Blank] dikes with a length of about 3,000 kilometers. The rest is mainly handled by the Work Relief Office of the Association, with a dike length of 4,398 kilometers, completing more than 18,100,000 cubic meters of earthwork, actually issuing more than 196,800 tons of wheat and grain, and spending more than 1,460,000 yuan on subsequent expenses. On average, 47 tons of wheat were issued for the construction of one kilometer of dike, and the cost was 330 yuan. The number of disaster workers was at least 300,000 and at most 900,000.

Dredging Water: The districts in eastern Henan, northern Anhui, and Lixiahe in northern Jiangsu have dredged 287 kilometers of river channels and straightened them, completing 3,540,000 cubic meters of earthwork, actually issuing 23,700 tons of wheat and grain, and spending more than 181,900 yuan on administrative expenses. On average, 83 tons of wheat were issued per kilometer and the cost was 634 yuan, because the river dredging is more difficult than the [Blank] embankment project. The scope of the Flood Relief Association's work relief is limited to earthwork. All other stone, earth, and concrete work is handled by local governments. However, after the floods in each province, financial resources were exhausted and fundraising was very reported. The flood defenses built by the bureaus in Henan and Anhui actually needed to add culverts and add stone work. Therefore, 24 culverts were built in the [Blank] wheat ration and 4 rivers and Ying rivers were added with stone and earthworks.

London Chinese Merchants Association

Launching the Eighteenth Fast

Proposing a monthly eighteenth day fast to contribute meal expenses to the military

And simultaneously restoring the Mingming Society lecture in the Eastern Provinces

The London Chinese Merchants Association recently sent a letter to the Municipal Assembly, which is to be forwarded to all organizations nationwide for their consideration. The Eastern Provinces have been lost for over a year now. Initially, we hoped the League of Nations could uphold justice and collectively condemn violence, but it has delayed and procrastinated, leaving us in a desperate situation. It is better to rely on ourselves than to seek help from others. Recalling the words of German Chancellor Bismarck, "International law is merely a matter of power, not justice. It is about blood and iron." If we do not lose our minds and become willing slaves of a fallen nation, we should deeply understand these words and strive together to restore our great land. Fortunately, the Northeastern Volunteer Army, with their unyielding spirit and perseverance, knowing they would rather be shattered jade than whole tiles, are fighting for the dignity of the people and for justice in the international community. If we cannot die on the battlefield alongside the Volunteer Army, how should we work together to provide support? Besides other donations and assistance, we suggest: (1) Every month on the eighteenth, compatriots worldwide should fast for one meal, using the feeling of hunger to remember the sacrifices of our Northeastern Volunteer Army compatriots and donate the saved expenses to the Volunteer Army. (2) On that day, at noon, wherever Chinese people are, they should stand facing the Northeast and swear three times: "I will do my utmost to restore the Three Northeastern Provinces to the Motherland!" (3) On that day, meetings and lectures should be held everywhere to commemorate the victims of the Japanese invasion and to arouse the determination of the people to seek revenge. Your Assembly is the leader of all organizations in our country, the head of the dragon looking forward. Now in managing, we specially suggest this to your Assembly, respectfully requesting that you consider adopting it, establish a method, and notify all Chinese organizations nationwide and worldwide to implement it consistently. The rise and fall of the nation is the responsibility of every individual. We are willing to work together for this. Respectfully submitted by: Wang Jingchou, Chairman of the London Chinese Merchants Association; Weng Shukuang, Document Officer; Li De, Accountant.

Report on the War Situation in the Northeast

A Cleverly Coded Telegram from Tang Yulin and Others Regarding Horse Rearing

Wang Delin's Forces Attack Jilin in Three Routes

The Northeastern Volunteer Army Support Association of this city received telegrams yesterday from Commander Tang Yulin and the General Headquarters of the National Salvation Army, reporting on the front-line combat situation. The telegrams are transcribed below:

Telegram from the Liaoning Headquarters (abridged): According to a telegram from Secretary Song Jingcheng of Kailu (22nd), based on a report from Liu Zhutang, Zhang Mianming's cavalry unit of over 500 men is stationed in the Haimiao area. 1,000 Japanese cavalry and a regiment of puppet troops with eight artillery pieces advanced to Gaoliban on the 18th. Li Fangting was forced to withdraw from Gaoliban due to pressure. Over 500 Mongolian soldiers are battling Liu Guitang's cavalry in the Tangjiayao Tuwangfu area. Please urgently send mortar shells and rifle bullets, etc. Aside from ordering a rapid replenishment, this is respectfully reported. Liaoning Headquarters, respectfully printed.

Another telegram stated (abridged): Recently received a telegram from Kailu Yang (22nd), reporting that according to a report from Regiment Commander Liu, Zhang Xia dispatched three detachments to cooperate with the Mongolian troops of Tu and Yetu, forcing our army to withdraw from the Gaoliban area. Because winter clothing has not arrived, they want to temporarily avoid their advance, hoping they will withdraw on their own. However, they repeatedly harass us, greatly hindering our forces. To be able to eliminate them and remove the Japanese bandits' puppet organizations and bases, there is a shortage of ammunition, especially 7.9mm bullets. Please quickly send supplies to resist the invaders, etc. Aside from ordering immediate transport and prioritized replenishment, this is respectfully reported. According to a telegram from the Tongjiang Commissioner, the rebel ships Liran and Jiangping defected on the evening of the 19th, and all Japanese advisors and pro-Japanese traitors were killed. This is specially reported. Liaoning Headquarters, printed.

Telegram from Tang Yulin (abridged above): Recently, Regiment Commander Dong reported by telegram on the 18th at noon that at (18th) o'clock, a Japanese plane circled several times over a mountain belonging to the Joseon region before flying east eight miles to a small village east of Joseon, dropping one bomb. It landed on the hillside of the 9th Company's defense line of the 213th Regiment, causing no damage. The plane flew east towards Joseon Street about 40 minutes later. At (17th) o'clock, the Joseon Temple troops fired over twenty artillery shells at the mountains seven miles south of Nanling. This is respectfully reported. Aside from ordering increased vigilance, this is specially reported. Commander Tang Yulin respectfully bows.

Telegram from the National Salvation Army (title abridged): Recently, according to a report from the Jilin Inspection Commissioner, on the 13th, Wang Desen's forces attacked Jilin in three routes: the central route taking Jiangmifeng, Liu's regiment taking A'geshiha on the left, and Zhang's regiment taking Gaoliangkou on the right. At eleven o'clock on the night of the 12th, a general offensive began. The fighting was fierce, and many Japanese soldiers died and retreated. Wang's army advanced to a place fifty miles from Jilin, etc. This is specially reported. According to a telegram from Kailu, based on a report from Liu Guitang's forces, on the 20th, the Japanese side dispatched three detachments to attack Gaoliban, and contact has been made. However, Liu's forces are lacking 7.9mm bullets. Please urgently transport the needed supplies. General Headquarters of the National Salvation Army, respectfully bows.

The Municipal Volunteer Army Rises Again

Deciding to Reorganize and March Out of the Pass to Recover Lost Territory

Preparatory Committee for Departure to the Northeast Established Yesterday

Notification to Dispersed Comrades to Gather in Shanghai

Since the "September 18th" Incident, the citizens of Shanghai have been indignant at Japan's barbarity and grieved at the loss of territory. Consequently, the Shanghai Citizens' United Association gathered patriotic volunteers to organize the Municipal Volunteer Army, preparing to march out of the Pass to fight the enemy and recover lost territory. Later, due to the sudden outbreak of the "January 28th" Shanghai Incident, they joined the 19th Route Army and participated in the battle against the Japanese in Zhabei and Wusong. The Municipal Volunteer Army participated in the war of resistance, demonstrating remarkable achievements in the history of defeating the enemy. After the signing of the ceasefire agreement, Brigadier General Weng Zhaoyuan led them to Wuxi for camp training. Later, through the efforts of Cai Tingkai and others, they were disbanded and sent back to Shanghai, leaving these passionate young people with a heart to serve the country but nowhere to use their abilities, which is deeply regrettable. Now, for several months, as the national crisis has become increasingly severe, patriotic volunteers, mindful of the principle that the rise and fall of the nation is the responsibility of every individual, could not bear to stand by and watch indifferently. Therefore, several comrades jointly initiated, convening former classmates, and decided to reorganize and march out of the Pass to recover lost territory. The comrades of the army held a meeting yesterday (27th) at 9:00 AM at the Datu Temple on North Chengdu Road in the International Settlement to discuss preparatory matters. Those who attended included Zhang Xifan, Huang Shuzhao, Zhang Qihong, Gu Jusheng, Peng Xiuchen, Gong Zhongda, Wang Haiqing, Zhang Yun, Wu Xiaozhou, Gu Guorong, Wang Zhongyi, Leng Tiqiang, Qu Xixi, Ling Derui, Zhu Erqing, Zhang Hao, Jia Fugui, Zhou Yong, Ye Yizhou, Wang Ruizeng, Ku Haisheng, Shen Yimin, Cheng Yangtian, Ku Shurong, Li Jinsheng, Gu Songyun, Liu Zhongwu, Jiang Wenxu, Lu Peiwen, Huang Xiebing, Lu Yong, and over fifty others. Chen Guangxiang, Wang Zhaocheng, Liu Zhongying, Wu Banlu, and Sun Bin, members of the Volunteer Army Committee of the Shanghai Citizens' United Association, also attended to provide guidance. The meeting officially began with nine rings of the bell. Wang Zhaocheng was elected as chairman and Chen Guangxiang as secretary. After the ceremony and discussion, the chairman announced the purpose of the meeting. Wang Haiqing, Chen Guangxiang, and others reported on the initiation and preparation process, and then discussed the implementation plan. Six key points were agreed upon: (1) The name was set as "Shanghai Municipal Volunteer Army Departure to the Northeast Preparatory Committee." (2) Wang Haiqing, Wang Zhongyi, Gu Guorong, Leng Tiqiang, Zhang Yunhua, Zha Zhida, Cheng Yangtian, Liu Zhongwu, and Peng Xiuchen were elected as the nine members of the preparatory committee. (3) A request will be submitted to the Volunteer Army Committee of the Shanghai Citizens' United Association to oversee the implementation. (4) The Datu Temple will be temporarily used as the registration office. (5) Newspapers and communication methods will be used to gather comrades for organization. (6) All matters related to advancement will be handled by the preparatory committee. The meeting adjourned at 1:00 PM.

Chinese Women's Association for Relief of Northeastern Compatriots

Yesterday's Founders' Discussion Meeting

The Chinese Women's Association for Relief of Northeastern Compatriots, initiated by the wives of Li Jishen, Sun Ke, and Wu Tiecheng, held a founders' discussion meeting at the YWCA on Nanjing Road at 2:00 PM on the 27th. Attendees included Mrs. Wu Tiecheng, Dr. Zheng Yuxiu, Central Committee member He Xiangning's representative Ma Jingyun, Mrs. Gan Naikuan, Mrs. Feng Jiasui, Mrs. Li Liejun's representative Bei Limin, Women's Bank President Yan Shuhe, Mrs. Jian of the Nanyang Tobacco Company, Ms. Zhang Lianying representing Liu Wang Liming, Principal Wang Xiaoying of Wuben Girls' Middle School, Mrs. Liu Renhang, and over twenty others. (Mrs. Li Jishen was ill, and Mrs. Sun Ke was unable to attend due to business.) Dr. Zheng Yuxiu was appointed chairman and opened the meeting as scheduled. Chairman Ms. Wang Xiaoying delivered the opening remarks, stating that the association was originally proposed by Mrs. Li Jishen, who is now bedridden in the hospital due to overwork. She entrusted the chairman to express that the Northeast is a part of the whole country and as important as other provinces. For the sake of national salvation and self-preservation, no one can ignore the plight of our Northeastern compatriots. Women account for two-fifths of the country's population, and we have the same passion and sympathy. Due to physiological reasons, we cannot rush to the battlefield, but we have many opportunities to contribute to the rear, such as relief, economic support, and propaganda. Does our women's community have the power to take on these tasks? Premier Sun once told us that unity is power. How can we unite? We must have an organization to unite. Hopefully, the establishment of this association will be the driving force of our women's power and the center of our women's power. Then, Ms. Song Zhennu reported on the preparation process with Mrs. Li. The speaker choked with emotion when mentioning the suffering of the Northeastern compatriots, and the attendees wept. Next, the discussion items were: (1) determining the name of the association, (2) discussing the constitution, (3) designating the attendees today as members of the preparatory committee, and selecting nineteen people from among them as executive committee members, (4) leaving the remaining items to the executive committee for collective discussion and responsible preparation. The following nineteen people were elected on the spot: Mrs. Li Jishen, Mrs. Sun Ke, Mrs. Chen Zhenru, Mrs. Wu Tiecheng, Mrs. Shi Liangcai, Dr. Zheng Yuxiu, Mrs. Du Yuesheng, Mrs. Gan Naiyi, Mrs. Jian, Mrs. Deng Jiayan, Mrs. Liu Renhang, Central Committee member Ms. He Xiangning, Women's Bank President Yan Shuhe, Song Zhen, Shu Zhirui, Wang Xiaoying, Wei Ying, Ouyang Huizhen, and Lu Huimin, and other ladies. Finally, Chairman Zheng delivered a speech, saying that the spirit of today's meeting is excellent, and she hopes that our women's community will strive to unite and create a large-scale and lasting organization to fight for the country. We must know that the progress of a country depends on whether the thinking of the women in that country is progressive. Now that the country is in such a difficult situation, we women must quickly work hard and save the country quickly.

Yesterday Morning's Memorial Service for Hu Hongji

More than Twenty Organizations

Held at the Lake Society

Hu Hongji, the former Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, tragically lost his life on the 15th of last month on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway near Haiyan. The news of his passing caused widespread grief and mourning. Yesterday, starting at 10:00 AM, the Shanghai Municipal Government, various bureaus and departments, as well as medical organizations and schools in the city, held a memorial service at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road. Over a thousand people attended, all with sorrowful expressions.

The venue was decorated with pine and cypress archways outside the main entrance, inscribed with "Memorial Service for Director Hu Hongji." Inside the hall, a portrait of Hu Hongji hung in the center, flanked by the national flag and party flag. Dozens of flower baskets were placed in front of the portrait, and wreaths from various sectors were arranged on both sides of the stage. Condolence banners were hung around the hall, creating a simple yet solemn atmosphere.

Notable attendees yesterday included Mayor Wu and various bureau chiefs, Central Committee members Zhang Zhijiang, Zhang Qun, Sun Ke (represented by Chen Jianru), Tang Haian, Yang Hu, Wang Jingqi, Li Xuanguo, Hu Gangfu, Yin Rugeng, Yan Fuqing, Guo Shun, Li Denghui, Niu Huisheng, Xu Peihuang, Liu Ruiheng, Yu Jun, Zhang Chouyong, and representatives from various organizations. Representatives from the International Health Bureau included Haas and Gai Ansen. The League of Nations Health Department representative was Bao Xike. The representative from the Peking Union Medical College was De. The representative from the Foreign Affairs Office was Zhang Meng. The representative from the Postal Administration was Zhang Xiangru. The representative from the Security Bureau was Zeng Keguang. The representative from the Shanghai Medical College was Fang Zichuan. The representative from the Chinese Medical Association was Zhu Hengbi, among over a thousand attendees. A Glimpse of the Condolence Banners Thousands of condolence banners were presented by various sectors. Noteworthy and interesting examples that attracted the attention of guests included: (Wu Tiecheng) "His reputation filled the south of the Yangtze, his meritorious service was diligent. In these difficult times, he worked for the common good. The news of his sudden passing echoes across the sea, a sudden and tragic event, leaving his colleagues in sorrow." (Huang Fu) "We cherish his benevolent care for health, and admire his lofty character like a high mountain. His scholarship and conduct were outstanding. In this difficult time, the loss of such a talented person is deeply saddening, both for the public and for personal reasons." (Dai Jitao) "His fame was well-deserved, his heroic spirit of braving the sea is reminiscent of Dan'an. His righteous writings live on, his tragic death like a overturned chariot reminds of Boyi." (Liu Yazi) "He sought health for the entire city, his medicine-free approach should ultimately reach the upper realms. He dedicated himself to administration, may this incident be a warning for future endeavors." (Yang Quan) "Death takes many forms. Zhi Mo met his end in the sky, and now you meet yours in a car accident. Wherever your interests lie, may that be your final resting place. Your responsibility is like that of Song Liao, with Manchuria falling to the enemy and the nation in peril. The landscape is like a painting, let us all compose a poem to summon your soul." (Rong Zongjing) "The two characters of 'health' are welcomed by the public. Even across the Huangpu River, your plans were detailed and your achievements are evident. A tragic change in the morning, lamenting your fleeting youth. From now on, on the Haiyan road, those who come and go will feel deep sorrow and remembrance." (Mu Xiangyue) "Rich in health expertise, a renowned doctor, years of major municipal construction. Your teachings were deeply influential. Life and death are fleeting, the songs of Chu are doubly sorrowful." (Zhang Dingfan) "Just relying on health to strengthen the nation, why did you embark on a long journey to the east?" (Zhang Zhijiang) "People grieve for the fall of a literary star, and the river echoes with lamenting sounds." (Sun Jiangyi) "Creation is unjust, why such drunkenness of heaven? A long talent cut short, where shall your soul find peace?"

Organizations Participating in the Memorial Shanghai Municipal Government and its various bureaus and departments, National Shanghai Medical College, National Tongji University, Tongde Medical College, Southeast Medical College, Bethel Vocational School and Renhe Midwifery School, Cihang Midwifery School, Dade Midwifery School, Tongji Midwifery School, Sino-German Midwifery School, Huizhu Women's Midwifery School, Chinese Medical Association, Chinese National Pharmaceutical Association, Chinese National Medical Association, Shenzhou Medical Association, Shanghai Nanguo Medical Association, Chinese Red Cross Society, Shanghai Physicians' Association, Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, Shanghai National Pharmaceutical Association.

Order of the Ceremony 1. Play funeral music. 2. All stand in silence. 3. The chairman lays flowers. 4. Pay three bows to the former Director Hu. 5. Official reads the memorial oration. 6. The chairman delivers a eulogy. 7. Report on the life and deeds of the former Director Hu. 8. Report by the wife of Director Hu. 9. Speech by Director Liu. 10. Speech by Lai Qi. 11. Family expresses gratitude. 12. Play funeral music. End of the ceremony.

Memorial Oration for Mr. Hu Following the ceremony, Wen Yuanshuo, representing the Municipal Government, read the memorial oration, stating: "On the seventh day of October in the twenty-third year of the Republic of China, Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of Shanghai, along with various bureaus, departments, agencies, schools, organizations, and people from all walks of life, respectfully offer incense, flowers, wine, and sacrifices to the spirit of Dr. Hu Hongji, the Director of the Health Bureau. Mr. Hu, since childhood, showed intelligence and devoted himself to learning. He was respectful, harmonious, taciturn, and handled matters with order and principle, earning the respect of all. He participated in the war in Europe, braving dangers and hardships. He studied abroad and reached the pinnacle of his field. Upon returning to his homeland, he embodied virtue, kindness, gentleness, and respectfulness. He moved to Shanghai, taking up his post with dedication. For seven years, he worked diligently. Suddenly, news of his tragic death came, leaving us devastated. The pillar has collapsed, and the loss is heartrending. His mother is in the hall, his wife and children are beside us. Colleagues are silent, filled with sorrow. Thinking of the past, tears stream down our faces. Let us follow in your footsteps, offering a white horse and a carriage. May your spirit find peace. Alas, mournful cries still echo."

Chairman's Eulogy Mayor Wu Tiecheng, after the official read the memorial oration, delivered a eulogy, stating: "The former Director Hu, with his decade-plus of dedicated research in health science and his seven years of experience in managing the city's health affairs, could have continued his efforts to bring even greater health benefits to the citizens of our city. The sudden and tragic news is shocking. It not only means that the Municipal Government has lost a capable assistant, but also that the citizens of the city will suffer a major blow. After the January 28th Incident this year, corpses littered the fields in Jiangwan and Wusong. People initially feared that a major epidemic was imminent. However, the former Director Hu worked tirelessly to plan and implement epidemic prevention measures after the end of the war. Therefore, the mortality statistics for this year are lower than in other places. This is all due to the efforts of the former Director Hu. Therefore, on behalf of the various agencies, schools, and organizations in this city, I offer my deepest condolences to the spirit of the former Director Hu." In addition, speeches were given by Director Liu Ruiheng of the National Health Administration and representatives of the Chinese Medical Association, with their content summarized for brevity.

Report on Life Story Originally, the wife of Director Hu was scheduled to report on Mr. Hu's life. However, due to her extreme grief and inability to speak, Mr. Hu's younger brother delivered the report, stating: "Mr. Hu began his dedication to medical life after the founding of the Republic of China. During the European War, he went to Europe to assist the American Red Cross. After returning to China, he once served as a professor and managed epidemic prevention efforts in various places. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China, with the introduction of the American Ran Ansen, he went to the United States to study, and in the thirteenth year he obtained his doctorate. After returning to China, he served as the director of the Qingdao Puji Hospital. In the fourteenth year, he resigned and returned home. During the era of the Shanghai-Songhu Merchant Port, Mr. Hu served as the Deputy Director of the Shanghai-Songhu Health Bureau. After the revolutionary army recovered Shanghai, Mr. Hu was promoted to Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, which he held for seven years. The occurrence of this unfortunate incident has caused extreme grief to the entire family. We express our gratitude to all sectors for their condolences."

Family's Expression of Gratitude The family representative, Hu's elder brother Banming, stated: "My younger brother Hongji suffered an unexpected tragedy. The Municipal Government, various bureaus, departments, organizations, and schools have remembered my brother's humble efforts and diligent work in Shanghai over the years. They initiated this memorial service, and we are deeply grateful to the party and government officials, representatives, and all relatives and friends who have honored us with their presence, bestowed generous donations, and composed grand elegies. The family is deeply saddened and distraught. My nephews and nieces are young and ignorant of protocol. Their failure to properly express gratitude is a great fault. We will deeply engrave the kindness of all in our hearts, inform our nephews and nieces, instill in them a sense of responsibility, use this support for their education, so that they can establish themselves and carry on his legacy, to repay your great kindness. "According to the family representative, Mr. Hu had three sons, named Weisheng, Zaisheng, and Ansheng, and two daughters, named Feifei and Xiaomei. The oldest is only five years old, and the youngest is still being nursed. The atmosphere was very somber. After the ceremony in the morning, the condolence visits began in the afternoon. It is reported that the collected donations will be used for the education of Mr. Hu's children.

Local News 2

Robbery at Jifu Lane, Ningbo Road

One Robber Killed, One Captured

More than Thirty People Confined to the Back Room for Two Hours as Five Robbers Searched and Plundered. A Large Group of Detectives Suddenly Burst in, Leading to a Fierce Battle, Leaving Bullet Marks on the Walls.

Yesterday afternoon around 7:00 PM, a robbery occurred at Jifu Lane on Ningbo Road. Detectives apprehended the robbers on the spot, leading to a fight in which one robber was killed and another captured. The details from the investigation are as follows:

Five Well-Dressed Robbers Jifu Lane on Ningbo Road is the former name, now known as No. 457 Lane. The lane primarily consists of commercial establishments. The ten-house shikumen, a three-story building, has Yuan Yu Cotton Cloth Shop and Yongchang Shop on the right side of the ground floor, and Ju Kang Shop on the left. The upper floors are rented by the San Yi New Motor Silk Weaving Factory and Guangfu Chang Shop. Managers of each shop have their families residing in the premises, totaling about thirty people. At approximately 5:45 PM yesterday afternoon, five young men, all well-dressed, suddenly arrived at the building. One of them closed the main gate, two went straight upstairs, and two others entered the Yuan Yu Shop on the right side of the ground floor. The employees of the shop were having dinner. Seeing the young men enter, they assumed they were there for business. However, the two men pulled out guns, forbidding anyone from making a sound, and drove all the employees into the back room of the shop. At the same time, the two men upstairs also forced all the people upstairs downstairs and confined them into the same back room.

Search and Plunder for About Two Hours After the robbers confined all the men, women, and children into the back room, they demanded the keys to the silver safes from the employees of each shop. Only Yuan Yu Shop handed over a key to an ordinary silver safe. The robbers assigned one person to guard the door of the back room with a gun, two searched and plundered downstairs, and two returned upstairs, ransacking every drawer and box. From 5:45 PM to 7:20 PM, the search continued. As there was little of value in each shop, the robbers were not satisfied and re-entered the back room, intimidating the people once again. The quarrel became protracted. One of the robbers fired a shot into the ground as a warning, but the employees remained unmoved. Seeing that the demonstration was ineffective, one of the robbers turned to the Yuan Yu Shop employees, threatening them to hand over another silver safe key. The employees claimed it was with the manager, so the robbers remained unsuccessful.

One Robber Dies, One Captured Just as the conflict was ongoing, a large group of detectives arrived outside the gate. Seeing that the gate was tightly closed, they knocked on the door. Hearing the sound, the robbers panicked. As they turned to flee, the detectives broke down the door. Half of them rushed into the left side room, finding it empty, so they entered the right side room. The two robbers in the room had already retreated. Each began to fire at the detectives. One robber took advantage of the chaos and ran straight out of the gate, escaping down the lane. Another robber was about to flee when he was spotted by a detective. The detective ordered him to stop. The robber was captured. At the same time, one of the robbers guarding the back room saw that the situation had been exposed and planned to flee. He hid near the door and fired at the detectives, resisting arrest. The detectives fired back, exchanging fire for over thirty shots. The robber was shot and fell to the ground. The two robbers upstairs heard the gunfire and realized that things were going badly. They fled to the rooftop, escaping across the roofs. When another group of detectives went upstairs, they were too late to pursue them.

Statistics on Losses in Each Shop After the detectives killed one robber and captured another, they released the people from the back room and, together, inspected the losses in each room. Ju Kang lost about 100 yuan, Yuan Yu lost about 30 yuan, and Yongchang, because no one was there, was not robbed. San Yi New Motor Silk Weaving Factory lost three bank notes and 30 yuan in cash. Guangfu Chang suffered the heaviest losses, with 50 yuan in cash and jewelry worth about 800 yuan stolen. The walls of the back room were covered in bullet marks, and the glass in front of a cabinet was shattered. The robber who fell to the ground was dead. His body lay across the doorway of the right side room, covered in blood. He was about 27 or 28 years old, wearing a wool hat and a long gray plain Mao Ge robe. Upon inspecting his body, there were six bullet wounds. A portion of the stolen goods was found. The police station transported the body to the Fei Lun Road coroner's office and took the captured robber into custody. Other detectives were dispatched to pursue the remaining robbers. The deceased robber was named Xiao Sanbao.

Han Traitor Murder Case

Continued Interrogation of the Murderer of Ji Jintang

After the January 28th Incident, the area under the jurisdiction of District Three, Section Five of the Hu Jia Mu Bridge and Xiangyan Bridge in Hongkou was the first to be occupied by the Japanese army. A group of Jiangbei hooligans willingly became traitors, joining the Japanese military headquarters to serve as accomplices, taking the opportunity to rob merchants of their property and opening opium dens and gambling dens in the area. Hu Lifu, Wang Du, and others were the leaders, including those from the entire Zhabei area. Those in the Hu Jia Mu Bridge area, according to the accusations of Ji Wu and others, included Wang Shubao, Wang Thirtyzi, and Zheng Xiaoheizi (aka Zheng Baocheng), three or four people in total. They obtained pistols issued by the Japanese and engaged in bullying their compatriots, confiscating the belongings of passersby to fill their own pockets. Later, they opened gambling dens. Ji Zhongtang, a former detective who had just been released from prison and was also from Jiangbei, went to the area hoping to share in the profits based on his previous position. However, he was shot and killed by Wang and others in a teahouse. This occurred in mid-February of this year. The death of Ji Zhongtang was of no more significance than that of an ant. The Japanese military police immediately ordered his body to be collected and naturally protected the perpetrators. Ji's family and apprentices remained silent, requesting the local bailiff Xu Jinlin to have the body examined at the Nanshi District Court the next day and accuse Wang and the other two. They were instructed to arrest them after the war had ended. After the ceasefire agreement was reached and the lost territory was gradually recovered, all the traitors lost their protection. Wang Thirtyzi, Zheng Xiaoheizi, and others used their ill-gotten wealth to open shops in the area, pretending to be honest merchants, causing righteous merchants to grumble about the world of evildoers. However, their ostentatious behavior attracted the attention of the authorities. Therefore, the three criminals urgently sought a private settlement with Ji Zhongtang's apprentices, who had reported them at the time, claiming that they did not recognize them and that it was someone else who committed the crime. However, Ji's wife, Ji Wu, had already reported the case to the court and District Three, Section Five. The police discovered that Zheng Xiaoheizi was celebrating his mother's birthday at home last month and went to arrest him on the spot. The other two Wangs escaped. Zheng was immediately sent to the Public Security Bureau and then to the District Court for investigation. Yesterday, he was interrogated again by the prosecutor. Zheng's family filed a petition claiming he was wronged and requesting bail, which the court naturally denied. The court also ordered the arrest of Wang Shubao and Wang Thirtyzi to be brought to justice.

The Flashlight Shone

Scaring the Extortionist into Capture

Reaching into the Trash Can

His Face Lit Up with Joy

Just as He Was About to Flee

Detectives Surrounded Him from All Sides

Gordong Road No. 161, Shanghai Beer Factory, chief carter Gao Yushu, received two threatening letters starting on the 5th of this month, intending to extort 500 yuan. On the 22nd, he received a third letter, instructing him to send a representative with the money to the trash can on the telegraph pole at No. 27 Lane, Anren Street, Min'guo Road, in the Chinese district between 8:00 PM and 9:00 PM the next evening. Someone would come to pick it up. If he did not comply, they would resort to extreme measures. Gao took the letter and reported the situation to the Putuo Road Police Station. The police chief dispatched Chinese Detective Wu Changkai and Bao Detective Zhang Changkun, along with detectives from the Public Security Bureau, to guard the location. However, because the lane was quite long and there were no places to hide on all sides, the detectives decided that Detective Wu would obtain the consent of a mansion opposite the telegraph pole in the lane to hide in the room and observe. Any movement would be signaled by a flashlight. The other detectives would be scattered around in ambush. They put newspapers in a paper bag to make it look like 200 yuan and put it in the trash can. After waiting for a long time, at 8:30 PM, two robbers arrived, pacing back and forth in the lane. Seeing that there was no one around, one robber reached into the trash can, took out the paper bag, and his face lit up with joy. Just as he was about to flee, Detective Wu showed no mercy and shone the flashlight. Detectives gathered from all sides and arrested the two robbers. They were first taken to the Public Security Bureau for detention, and then taken back to the police station the next morning. They were then transferred to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Wu Zhen took the stand and first questioned the defendants about their names, ages, and hometowns. The defendants claimed their names were Li Hongqi (the one who reached in and took the money), from Tianjin, and Zhou Fabao, from Huzhou. Then, the police lawyer Wang Tang stepped forward and stated the above situation, requesting an extension and detention of the two defendants. Judge Wu granted the request and ordered Li and Zhou to be detained for seven days for further interrogation.

Children Playing with Fire Causes Disaster

An Accident Occurred Last Night in Ma'an Lane

Two of Three Children Burned to Death

Wang Gu, a thirty-two-year-old woman from Suzhou, lived with her three daughters in a garret at 641 Ma'an Lane, Maurice Road, in the Public Concession. The eldest daughter, Gendi, was eleven years old, the second daughter, Nuannuan, was five years old, and the youngest daughter, Qiaofeng, was only two years old. Last night around 10:00 PM, Nuannuan was hungry and wanted a snack. Wang went out to buy something. Only the three children remained in the room. Gendi liked to play with matches. After lighting them, she lit the kerosene lamp, making it very bright. Inadvertently, the kerosene lamp fell on the bedding and suddenly caught fire. The curtains and mats were mostly flammable materials. In an instant, smoke filled the room, flames shot out, and the fire broke through the roof. By the time Wang returned home, the fire was already out of control. Nuannuan, though young, was quick-witted and escaped the fire, preserving her life. The two older and younger children were buried in the fire, their heads charred, a tragic sight to behold. The fire department arrived in vehicles to put out the fire, extinguishing it after some time. The bodies of the children were sent to the Bao Lung Hospital in a hearse to await examination.

Children Lost in Zhabei Are Frequent

Three Women from Wanxiang Claim to Have Purchased Them

Kidnapping has been rampant in Zhabei recently, with missing boys and girls becoming an almost daily occurrence. Therefore, anyone with children is living in constant fear. The details known yesterday are as follows: 1. The Cai Shunxing Bamboo Shop at 177 Datong Road lost two boys: Cai Baogen, five years old, wearing a cotton robe made in the factory, a long floral striped cloth coat, a white cloth shirt underneath, floral wool trousers, and black shoes; and De'gen, three years old, wearing a striped cloth jacket, a red floral foreign cloth cotton coat, striped cloth trousers, floral socks, and floral shoes. Both children have scars on their feet. 2. The Yuanqingxiang Cigarette and Paper Shop at 263 Menggu Road lost a three-year-old boy with a scar on his left eye, wearing a blue plaid cotton-padded jacket and black rubber shoes. 8. An eight-year-old boy named Xiao Hong went missing at the intersection of Hanzhong Road and Huasheng Road, wearing a yellow wool serge gown and wool trousers. 9. The Wu Xudong family at the entrance of Hengtong Lane, Hengtong Road, lost a three-year-old boy named Wu Thirtyzi, wearing a duckbill cap, gray cotton-padded jacket and trousers made in the factory, and a straight wool gown. He was carried away by a man about twenty years old wearing a Japanese hat.

Yesterday morning around 11:00 AM, city Public Security Bureau Water Patrol Team officer Bian Chunlin and others were patrolling the river to the Ning Shao Wharf at 16th Shed, when they saw the Wanxiang Steamer docked there and not yet sailing. They boarded the ship to conduct an inspection. They found three Fujian women, Wang Tang, Ding Wang, and Li Ren, each holding an infant in swaddling clothes in the steerage. Seeing the police arrive, they immediately looked flustered and suspicious. When asked about the origin of the children, they were evasive. They were immediately taken to the team. When Zhu, the team leader, preliminarily interrogated the case, Wang Tang and others claimed that the children they were holding were all purchased from the countryside in Pudong. They were now planning to take them back to their hometown as their own sons. Because the matter concerned trafficking in persons, they were ordered to prepare a document and send it to the bureau for further investigation.

Fang Rongzhou's Daughter

Sues for Inheritance

To Divide 300,000 into Six Shares

Requesting Investigation of the Yuanyuan Sugar Trading House Accounting Books

The Fang family of Zhenhai is known for its wealth. They operate many businesses in Shanghai, Hangzhou, and other ports. The Yuanyuan Sugar Trading House in Shanghai was founded by Fang Rongzhou. Rongzhou had four sons and three daughters: Meng Ruinian, Zhong Funian, Shu Zunian, and Ji Wennian. Funian and Zunian died early. Xinru left behind two sons, named Zigang and Ziqin. As for the three daughters, the eldest, Zhiqing, is also deceased. The second, Jinqing, married a Chen. The youngest, Youqing, married into the Fang family. Rongzhou passed away in the early years of the Republic of China, leaving behind an inheritance of hundreds of thousands. In the previous year, Ruinian and his brothers, uncles, and nephews divided it into four parts. At that time, laws on women inheriting property had already been promulgated, but Ruinian and others did not legally distribute Jinqing's and Youqing's rights. Recently, Youqing hired lawyer Wang Shizong to file a lawsuit against Ruinian and others in the First Special District Court, demanding that the 300,000 inheritance be divided equally into six shares and requesting that the accounting books of the Yuanyuan Sugar Trading House be examined to prove that the capital of the house belonged to Rongzhou. The defendant also hired a lawyer to argue that the plaintiff had no right to divide the property. The First Special Court repeatedly opened court to hear the case. The other day, Judge Qiao opened the court. After the plaintiff and defendant lawyers argued, the judge announced that the sentence would be announced at a later date.

News from the National Federation of All Circles for National Salvation

Sending Personnel North to Comfort the Troops;

Telegram Urging Sichuan Army to Cease Internal Strife

Since its establishment on the 30th of last month, the National Federation of All Circles for National Salvation has been working exceptionally hard for national salvation. Because the righteous armies outside the passes are fighting bloody battles against the enemy in the icy and snowy lands, striving for the survival of the motherland, the Federation has specially dispatched directors Zhang Jie and Feng Guo, and others, carrying goods, to offer comfort and to conduct an on-the-ground investigation of the anti-Japanese situation of the righteous armies. They already departed north on the Beijing-Shanghai express train at 7:00 AM yesterday (the 26th). Those who saw them off included more than one hundred people from various public organizations in Shanghai, such as the Chinese Women's Rights Movement Grand Alliance, and Federation directors Zhang Junguang and Zuo Hua. It is heard that this trip will take two months before they can return to Shanghai.

Furthermore, it is reported that the Federation, in light of the unresolved Sichuan war, specifically telegraphed urging for cessation of hostilities, stating: Sichuan (title omitted). Your area and the salt wells are being brutally invaded and occupied by Japan. All Chinese are filled with indignation and heartache, and are willing to go together to face the national crisis and reduce our daily meals to that end. Now, instead of saving the country from danger, your armies are engaging in fratricidal strife, harming each other like beans and stalks, leading to ridicule from foreign nations and providing ammunition for their attacks. Our Federation, with a sincere heart, earnestly advises your armies to quickly cease internal strife, reorganize your forces, and jointly resist the brutal Japanese for the sake of the country and the nation (remainder omitted).

Furthermore, the Federation telegraphed Jiang Guangnai in Fuzhou, stating (in brief): Your army's current suppression of bandits in Fujian will undoubtedly lead to significant achievements in the renewal of Fujian's administration. However, the reorganization of the Fujian provincial government is being delayed. At this time of suppressing bandits and resisting foreign aggression, military and political affairs should naturally be carried out in full cooperation. It is hoped that you, sir, will overcome all difficulties and promptly recommend individuals from Fujian province who possess revolutionary history and are respected by the public to serve as chairman, and that you will join with overseas Chinese in the construction of politics and economics.

Donation to Disaster Victims in Three Provinces

Jianghai Customs Inspection of Airplanes

China National Aviation Corporation Telegraphs Ministry for Instructions

The Shanghai-Hankou up and down line aircraft of the China National Aviation Corporation in this city have always been inspected by the military police of the Garrison Headquarters when taking off and landing at the airfield. Unexpectedly, the Jianghai Customs recently sent a letter to the company stating: According to orders from the Ministry of Finance, inspections will be carried out on aircraft takeoffs and landings, and the company is requested to provide a room at Longhua Airport for customs officials to work in. However, the company believes that aviation is not navigation and is not related to customs, so it is inconvenient to agree. It has telegraphed the Ministry of Transportation for instructions on how to proceed.

Ma Yinchu, a member of the Legislative Yuan's Economic Committee, replied yesterday to Xu Jingren, Wang Yiting, and Wang Xiaolai, the chairman and vice-chairmen of the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Disaster Area Relief Association, stating: I have received your kind instructions, as well as the Relief Association's declaration, brief regulations, and donation booklet. Native Association Holds Meeting to Assist. The Shanghai Fujian Native Association held its second executive committee meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. Xie Yinpo was publicly elected as chairman. In addition to reporting on the association's activities over the past week, the chairman first proposed that a committee be organized by linking up the Fujian natives in Shanghai to assist the Northeastern Righteous Army in raising large sums of money to provide assistance. It was publicly resolved that the committee would be established in the near future, and Xu Jigong, Huang Jiahu, Song Ziqing, Du Shuchen, Qiu Hanping, Chen Qun, Ouyuan Huai, Yang Shizhi, Yang Jingshi, Chen Kan, Li Wenbin, Xie Yinpo, Huang Xingge, Huang Yufu, Chen Daqi, Zhang Linong, and thirty-one others were appointed as executive committee members responsible for handling the matter. Subsequently, several motions were passed as follows: (1) The motion to establish a Fujian Public School to educate poor children was resolved to establish an education committee to be specifically responsible for planning and organizing. (2) The motion to issue boat tickets to Lin Zexing and fourteen other natives of Fujian in Shanghai to return to their hometown was resolved to be issued. (3) The motion to publicly decide on the resignation of Lin Shouchang and Huang Yufu as standing committee members, and Mao Yifeng as executive committee member, was resolved to be retained. The meeting then adjourned.

Jiangsu Rice Association Members' Annual Meeting

The Jiangsu Ning-Hu City and County Rice Industry Association held its second members' annual meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday at Cuixiutang. A total of 28 members from nine public associations attended. Zhao Zixin was publicly elected as chairman. After the formalities, the chairman reported that since the death of the association's chairman, Ye Huijun, no replacement has been appointed, which seems insufficient to show solemnity. At the last meeting, it was resolved to wait until the members' annual meeting to re-elect. Today is the annual meeting, and it is urgent to appoint a chairman to emphasize association affairs. It was also proposed to elect Mr. Yan Xiaoquan as a standing committee member, which was put to a vote. It was unanimously approved. As for the vacancy of the executive committee member, it was filled by the alternate executive committee member Pan Xianting. The vacancy of the alternate executive committee member was filled by Xu Shanqing, who had the next highest number of votes. As for the position of chairman, Zhao Zixin was elected through mutual election among the standing committee members. Regarding the Zhenjiang proposal to request the provincial government to implement the circulation of rice and grain from various provinces to alleviate farmers' difficulties, (resolved) The association had already telegraphed the provincial government to request instructions, but no reply has been received to date. A telegram should be sent again to request a prompt order to circulate rice and grain to provide relief. Furthermore, the Wujiang County proposal stated that the Shanghai rice and grain industry has changed to using weighing instruments to measure rice, and suggested that it would be difficult for the counties in the interior to change, so the proposal should be withdrawn. (Resolved) Send a letter to the Shanghai Soybean and Rice Industry Association for reference. Another Wujiang proposal suggested organizing a rice industry bank. (Resolved) This matter is of great importance, and in the current economic downturn, planning is difficult. We should wait for an opportunity to discuss it again. Subsequently, the preliminary income and expenditure accounts for the current year were reported, and members were urged to pay their dues for application.

Jiangxi Telegraph Agency Organized and Established

Branches Established in Beijing, Shanghai, Pinghan and other Places

The Jiangxi News Agency, the oldest and largest news agency in the province, recently expanded its internal organization and adopted the name "Jiangxi Telegraph Agency" in view of the closed nature of news in the province and the lack of a sound communication organization to the outside world. Fan Zhengbo was appointed as president. Mr. Fan is highly reputed in the domestic news industry, having served as a standing committee member of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters and president of the Shanghai Datong News Agency. He is currently a standing committee member of the Jiangxi Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee and director of the Jiujiang Republic Daily. He has excellent knowledge and extensive experience. All the staff of the agency are outstanding members of the domestic and provincial news industry. Preparations have been completed and the agency is scheduled to begin submitting articles on the 21st of this month. The internal organization and scope of work of the agency are described below. Internal Organization: In addition to Fan Zhengbo serving as president and editor, the important positions in each department have also been assigned as follows: (1) Editor-in-Chief: Li Zanhua, Editor: (Character missing) Qitian, Editor and Stenographer: Tu Chengli, (2) Interview Department Director: Zhang Douhang, Deputy Director and Editor: Gong Qinyu, Liu Bian, (3) General Affairs Department Director: Zhong Youzu, Sound Room Director: Zhong Huangan, etc. In addition, branches and correspondents have been established in various locations such as Beijing, Shanghai, Hankou, Pinghan, and in various counties and cities and institutions in the province. Scope of Work: After the expansion, the agency will not only issue mimeographed communications, but also send telegraphic and photographic news to newspapers across the country and in the province. In addition to the existing radio, the agency plans to install three more radios to receive and transmit domestic and international news.
